As a nod to Jordan's on-court play, the Men's Air Jordan Retro 5 Basketball Shoes were designed to look like a fighter plane. In the famed model, MJ earned his fourth consecutive scoring title, sixth All-Star appearance and led the Bulls to the Eastern Conference Finals.

Two Things!✌🏽
⠀
1. I love how slimming black makes me look and these nike Zoom 2k kicks will always be always be a favorite! I got these from finishline months ago, but they do still have them in stock if you’re interested!
⠀
2. I can’t wait until it’s safe to actually put on my outdoor clothes and hangout again! Although South Carolina is almost completely open again. It’s no where near safe to be out right now. Now I don’t watch the news or read the news articles (for my own peace of mind), but I just learned from my fam that there are 3,000 more cases in SC since last week. I made a quick run to the post office today and the amount of people I saw out at non-essential places was ridiculous! I honestly don’t know what people are thinking right now. But I know what Jay will be doing okay.💁🏽‍♀️

Two Things!✌🏽
⠀
1. I love how slimming black makes me look and these nike Zoom 2k kicks will always be always be a favorite! I got these from finishline months ago, but they do still have them in stock if you’re interested!
⠀
2. I can’t wait until it’s safe to actually put on my outdoor clothes and hangout again! Although South Carolina is almost completely open again. It’s no where near safe to be out right now. Now I don’t watch the news or read the news articles (for my own peace of mind), but I just learned from my fam that there are 3,000 more cases in SC since last week. I made a quick run to the post office today and the amount of people I saw out at non-essential places was ridiculous! I honestly don’t know what people are thinking right now.
